## Slide 2: üìö ‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß

### ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô

**‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 5: High-Level Architecture**
- ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ SOLID, DRY, KISS, YAGNI
- 3-Tier Architecture (Presentation ‚Üí Application ‚Üí Data)
- C4 Model Level 1-2 (Context & Container)

**‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 6: Design Patterns**
- **Creational:** Singleton, Factory
- **Structural:** Adapter, Facade
- **Behavioral:** Observer, Strategy, Command
- **Real-time:** Publisher-Subscriber, Circuit Breaker

**‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ (‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 7): Component Architecture**
- **C4 Level 3:** ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á Components ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô Containers
- **Component Design Principles:** High Cohesion, Loose Coupling
- **Component Communication:** Interface Design, Dependencies

**‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 8: Implementation Ready**
- **C4 Level 4:** Code Level Design
- **UML Diagrams:** Class, Sequence, Activity
- **API Specifications:** REST + WebSocket

## Slide 3: üß© Component ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£?

### ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Component

**üí° Component = ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞**

**üè† ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô:**
- **‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô** = ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö (Agent Wallboard System)
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ** = Components (‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ß, ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏ô, ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≥)
- **‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞** ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô

**üì¶ ‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Component ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ:**

**1. High Cohesion (‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô)**
- ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô component ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏µ
- ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

**2. Loose Coupling (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢)**
- ‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤ components ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢
- ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å

**3. Clear Interface (‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏ï‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô)**
- ‡∏°‡∏µ interface ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö components ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô
- ‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô (Encapsulation)

**4. Reusability (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ)**
- ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
- ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö implementation ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞

## Slide 4: üîÑ ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Design Patterns ‡∏™‡∏π‡πà Components

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ô‡∏≥ Patterns ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Components

**üíº ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ Patterns:**

**üè≠ Creational Patterns:**
- **Singleton** ‚Üí WebSocket Connection Manager Component
- **Factory** ‚Üí Message Factory Component

**üèóÔ∏è Structural Patterns:**
- **Adapter** ‚Üí Database Adapter Component  
- **Facade** ‚Üí API Facade Component

**üé≠ Behavioral Patterns:**
- **Observer** ‚Üí Event Broadcasting Component
- **Strategy** ‚Üí Authentication Strategy Component

**‚ö° Real-time Patterns:**
- **Publisher-Subscriber** ‚Üí Event Bus Component
- **Circuit Breaker** ‚Üí Resilience Component

**üéØ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏î:**
- **Pattern** = ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞
- **Component** = ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Patterns
- **Architecture** = ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á Components ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

**‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á:**
- **Observer Pattern** ‚Üí **Status Broadcasting Component**
- **Facade Pattern** ‚Üí **Dashboard API Component**
- **Singleton Pattern** ‚Üí **WebSocket Manager Component**

## Slide 5: üè¢ C4 Model Level 3 - Component Diagram

### ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Container ‡∏™‡∏π‡πà Component

**üìä C4 Model Recap:**
- **C1 (Context):** Agent Wallboard System ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà
- **C2 (Container):** Desktop App + API Server + Database
- **C3 (Component):** ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô Container ‚Üê **‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ**
- **C4 (Code):** Classes ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Functions ‚Üê ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤

**üéØ C3 Component Diagram ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á:**
- Components ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Container
- Interface ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Components
- Dependencies ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Data Flow
- ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô Design Patterns

**üìà ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç:**
- **‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Developers:** ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤, Task breakdown
- **‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Architects:** ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö design, Dependencies analysis  
- **‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Team Leads:** ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô, Resource allocation
- **‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö QA:** Test planning, Integration testing

**üîÑ Process:**

## Slide 6: üñ•Ô∏è Frontend Components - Agent Desktop App

### Components ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô Desktop Application (Electron.js)

**üì± Agent Desktop App Container ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Components:**

**üîê Authentication Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Login/Logout
- **Interface:** login(credentials), logout(), getCurrentUser()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Strategy Pattern (Local/SSO Authentication)
- **Dependencies:** Auth API, Session Manager

**üìä Status Management Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Agent (Available, Busy, Break, etc.)
- **Interface:** changeStatus(newStatus), getCurrentStatus(), getStatusHistory()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Observer Pattern (‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á status changes)
- **Dependencies:** Agent API, WebSocket Component

**üîî Real-time Notification Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á notifications ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö real-time
- **Interface:** showNotification(message), subscribeToEvents(), unsubscribe()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Observer Pattern (‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö events), Pub-Sub Pattern
- **Dependencies:** WebSocket Component, UI Framework

**üë§ Profile Management Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Agent
- **Interface:** getProfile(), updateProfile(data), getPreferences()
- **Dependencies:** Agent API, Local Storage

**üí¨ Message Display Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Supervisor
- **Interface:** displayMessage(message), markAsRead(), getMessageHistory()
- **Dependencies:** Message API, WebSocket Component

## Slide 7: üñ•Ô∏è Frontend Components - Supervisor Dashboard

### Components ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô Supervisor Web Dashboard

**üìä Dashboard Visualization Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞ Agents ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö real-time
- **Interface:** refreshDashboard(), filterAgents(), exportReport()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Observer Pattern (auto-refresh), Facade Pattern (‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•)
- **Dependencies:** Dashboard API, Chart Libraries, WebSocket

**üë• Agent Monitor Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞ Agent ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡∏Ñ‡∏•
- **Interface:** getAgentStatus(agentId), getAgentHistory(), sendMessage()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Observer Pattern (real-time updates)
- **Dependencies:** Agent API, WebSocket Component

**üì® Message Management Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á Agents (‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°)
- **Interface:** sendMessage(recipients, message), getBroadcastHistory()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Command Pattern (message commands), Factory Pattern (message types)
- **Dependencies:** Message API, Agent List Component

**üìà Reports Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô performance
- **Interface:** generateReport(criteria), exportToPDF(), scheduleReport()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Strategy Pattern (report types), Factory Pattern (export formats)
- **Dependencies:** Reporting API, Chart Libraries

**üéõÔ∏è Control Panel Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏° ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö
- **Interface:** updateTeamSettings(), manageAgents(), systemConfig()
- **Dependencies:** Admin API, Settings Component

## Slide 8: ‚öôÔ∏è Backend Components - API Server

### Components ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô Node.js API Server

**üîê Authentication Service Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö credentials ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á sessions
- **Interface:** authenticate(credentials), validateToken(token), refreshSession()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Strategy Pattern (auth methods), Singleton Pattern (session store)
- **Dependencies:** Database Adapter, JWT Library, Password Hash

**üë§ Agent Status Service Component**  
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞ Agents ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ status history
- **Interface:** updateStatus(agentId, status), getStatusHistory(), getCurrentTeamStatus()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Observer Pattern (broadcast changes), Command Pattern (status commands)
- **Dependencies:** Database Adapter, WebSocket Manager, Event Bus

**üì® Message Routing Service Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Supervisors ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Agents
- **Interface:** sendMessage(from, to, message), broadcastMessage(), getMessageHistory()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Factory Pattern (message types), Pub-Sub Pattern (routing)
- **Dependencies:** Database Adapter, WebSocket Manager, Message Queue

**üîå WebSocket Connection Manager Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ WebSocket connections ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ real-time communication
- **Interface:** handleConnection(socket), broadcastToClients(event, data), manageSubscriptions()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Singleton Pattern (one manager), Observer Pattern (connection events)
- **Dependencies:** Socket.IO Library, Event Bus, Session Manager

**üíæ Database Access Layer Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (MSSQL + MongoDB)
- **Interface:** query(sql), insertDocument(), updateRecord(), transaction()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Adapter Pattern (database types), Factory Pattern (connection types)
- **Dependencies:** Database Drivers, Connection Pool, Circuit Breaker

---

## Slide 9: üóÑÔ∏è Data Tier Components

### Components ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô Database Layer

**üóÉÔ∏è MSSQL Data Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ structured master data
- **‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£:** Agents, Teams, Users, System Configuration
- **Interface:** executeStoredProcedure(), executeSQLQuery(), manageTransactions()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Repository Pattern, Unit of Work Pattern
- **Features:** ACID properties, Referential integrity, Complex queries

**üçÉ MongoDB Data Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ real-time ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ log data
- **‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£:** Status Logs, Message History, Performance Metrics
- **Interface:** insertDocument(), findDocuments(), updateDocument(), aggregatePipeline()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Repository Pattern, Document Mapper
- **Features:** Fast writes, Flexible schema, Real-time analytics

**üîÑ Data Synchronization Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á MSSQL ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ MongoDB
- **Interface:** syncAgentData(), syncStatusUpdates(), reconcileData()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Adapter Pattern (data mapping), Observer Pattern (change detection)
- **Dependencies:** Both database components, Event Bus

**üíæ Connection Pool Manager Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ database connections ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û
- **Interface:** getConnection(dbType), releaseConnection(), monitorHealth()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Singleton Pattern, Object Pool Pattern
- **Features:** Connection reuse, Health monitoring, Load balancing

**üõ°Ô∏è Data Security Component**
- **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
- **Interface:** encrypt(data), decrypt(data), hashPassword(), auditAccess()
- **Pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:** Strategy Pattern (encryption methods), Decorator Pattern (security layers)
- **Dependencies:** Crypto libraries, Audit logs

---

## Slide 10: üîó Component Dependencies ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Relationships

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå Dependencies ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Components

**üìä Dependency Analysis:**

**üî∫ High-Level Dependencies (‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö):**
```
Frontend Components
    ‚Üì (HTTP/WebSocket)
Backend API Components  
    ‚Üì (Database queries)
Data Tier Components
```

**üîÑ Cross-Component Dependencies:**

**Frontend ‚Üí Backend:**
- Authentication Component ‚Üí Authentication Service
- Status Management ‚Üí Agent Status Service  
- Message Display ‚Üí Message Routing Service
- Dashboard ‚Üí Multiple backend services (via Facade)

**Backend Internal Dependencies:**
- WebSocket Manager ‚Üê All services (for real-time updates)
- Database Access Layer ‚Üê All services (for data operations)
- Authentication Service ‚Üê Other services (for authorization)

**Data Tier Dependencies:**
- MongoDB Component ‚Üê Real-time operations
- MSSQL Component ‚Üê Master data operations  
- Sync Component ‚Üê Both database components

**‚ö†Ô∏è Potential Issues:**
- **Circular Dependencies:** A depends on B, B depends on A
- **Too Many Dependencies:** One component depends on many others
- **Wrong Direction:** Lower layer depends on higher layer

**‚úÖ Best Practices:**
- **Dependency Injection:** Don't hardcode dependencies
- **Interface Segregation:** Depend on interfaces, not concrete classes
- **Layered Dependencies:** Higher layers depend on lower layers only

# ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 7: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ã‡∏≠‡∏ü‡∏ï‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πå - ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô (Part 2/4)
## Component Design Principles

---

## Slide 11: üèóÔ∏è Component Design Principles - High Cohesion

### ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ High Cohesion - ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏Ç‡πá‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô

**üí° High Cohesion = ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô Component ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß**

**üè† ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ß:**
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ:** ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏≤, ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á, ‡∏ï‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏¢‡πá‡∏ô, ‡∏≠‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ß ‚Üí ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ:** ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏≤, ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á, ‡πÇ‡∏ï‡πä‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô, ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏ú‡πâ‡∏≤ ‚Üí ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡∏õ‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏ô

**üíª ‡πÉ‡∏ô Agent Wallboard System:**

**‚úÖ High Cohesion Example - Authentication Component:**
```javascript
class AuthenticationComponent {
  // ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ authenticate
  login(credentials)           // ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö
  logout()                    // ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö  
  validateSession()           // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö session
  refreshToken()              // ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏ token
  hashPassword(password)      // ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™ password
  getCurrentUser()            // ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• user ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô
}
```
**‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß:** ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô

**‚ùå Low Cohesion Example - Mixed Component:**
```javascript
class MixedComponent {
  login(credentials)           // Authentication
  sendMessage(message)         // Messaging  
  generateReport()            // Reporting
  updateAgentStatus()         // Status Management
  connectDatabase()           // Database
}
```
**‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤:** ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á, ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å, ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å

**üéØ ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î High Cohesion:**
- **LCOM (Lack of Cohesion of Methods):** Method ‡πÉ‡∏ô class ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ instance variables ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô
- **Single Responsibility:** Component ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
- **Related Functionality:** Functions ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

---

## Slide 12: üîó Component Design Principles - Loose Coupling

### ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Loose Coupling - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢

**üí° Loose Coupling = Components ‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢, ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å**

**üè† ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏ü‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô:**
- **Loose Coupling:** ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å ‚Üí ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô
- **Tight Coupling:** ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‚Üí ‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏î

**üíª ‡πÉ‡∏ô Agent Wallboard System:**

**‚úÖ Loose Coupling Example:**
```javascript
// Authentication Service ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Database
class AuthenticationService {
  constructor(databaseAdapter) {  // Dependency Injection
    this.db = databaseAdapter;
  }
  
  async authenticate(credentials) {
    // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ interface ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á database ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô MSSQL ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ MongoDB
    return await this.db.findUser(credentials.username);
  }
}

// Database Adapter ‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î implementation
interface DatabaseAdapter {
  findUser(username): Promise<User>;
  saveUser(user): Promise<void>;
}
```

**‚ùå Tight Coupling Example:**
```javascript  
class AuthenticationService {
  async authenticate(credentials) {
    // Hardcoded dependency - ‡∏ú‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö MSSQL
    const connection = new MSSQL.connect('server=...');
    const result = await connection.query(`
      SELECT * FROM Users WHERE username = '${credentials.username}'
    `);
    // ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å MSSQL ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô MongoDB ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
  }
}
```

**üéØ ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏Ñ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Loose Coupling:**

**1. Dependency Injection**
- ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á dependencies ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô constructor ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ method parameters
- ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á dependencies ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô component

**2. Interface-based Programming**  
- ‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤ interfaces ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà concrete classes
- ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô implementation ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ

**3. Event-Driven Communication**
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ events ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÜ
- Publisher ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ subscriber ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á

---

## Slide 13: üîå Interface Segregation for Components

### ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Interface Segregation - ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å Interface

**üí° Interface Segregation = ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á Interface ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏á ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£**

**üè† ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≤:**
- **‡∏î‡∏µ:** ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏ß‡∏µ (‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏ß‡∏µ), ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏ó‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå (‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå)
- **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ:** ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á (‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏ß‡∏µ+‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå+‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á) ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å

**üíª ‡πÉ‡∏ô Agent Wallboard System:**

**‚úÖ Good Interface Segregation:**
```javascript
// ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å interface ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà
interface UserReader {
  getUser(id: string): Promise<User>;
  getUsersByTeam(teamId: string): Promise<User[]>;
}

interface UserWriter {
  createUser(user: User): Promise<void>;
  updateUser(id: string, updates: Partial<User>): Promise<void>;
  deleteUser(id: string): Promise<void>;
}

interface UserAuthenticator {
  authenticate(credentials: Credentials): Promise<AuthResult>;
  validateToken(token: string): Promise<boolean>;
}

// Component ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ interface ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
class DashboardComponent implements UserReader {
  // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏•‡∏ö/‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
}

class AdminComponent implements UserReader, UserWriter {
  // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô
}

class LoginComponent implements UserAuthenticator {
  // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ authenticate
}
```

**‚ùå Poor Interface Segregation:**
```javascript
// Interface ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ implement ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á
interface UserManager {
  getUser(id: string): Promise<User>;
  createUser(user: User): Promise<void>;
  updateUser(id: string, updates: Partial<User>): Promise<void>;
  deleteUser(id: string): Promise<void>;
  authenticate(credentials: Credentials): Promise<AuthResult>;
  generateReport(): Promise<Report>;
  sendEmail(email: Email): Promise<void>;
  backupData(): Promise<void>;
}

// ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á implement ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
class DashboardComponent implements UserManager {
  // ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á implement ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà getUser
  createUser() { throw new Error("Not supported"); }
  deleteUser() { throw new Error("Not supported"); }
  // ... ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏∞
}
```

## Slide 14: üíâ Dependency Injection Patterns

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Dependencies ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û

**üí° Dependency Injection = ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á dependencies ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô component**

**üè† ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£:**
- **DI:** ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ ‚Üí ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏ü‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£
- **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà DI:** ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏ü‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á ‚Üí ‡∏ú‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞

**üíª ‡πÉ‡∏ô Agent Wallboard System:**

**1. Constructor Injection**
```javascript
class AgentStatusService {
  constructor(databaseAdapter, eventBus, logger) {
    this.db = databaseAdapter;        // Database access
    this.eventBus = eventBus;         // Event publishing
    this.logger = logger;             // Logging
  }
  
  async updateStatus(agentId, status) {
    await this.db.updateAgentStatus(agentId, status);
    this.eventBus.publish('status_changed', {agentId, status});
    this.logger.info(`Agent ${agentId} changed to ${status}`);
  }
}

// ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
const service = new AgentStatusService(
  new DatabaseAdapter('MSSQL'),
  new EventBus(),
  new ConsoleLogger()
);
```

**2. Method Injection**
```javascript
class MessageService {
  sendMessage(message, messageSender) {
    // ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö dependency ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô method parameter
    return messageSender.send(message);
  }
}

// ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
messageService.sendMessage(message, new EmailSender());
messageService.sendMessage(message, new SMSSender());
```

**3. Interface Injection (Property Injection)**
```javascript
class DashboardComponent {
  // Properties ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞ inject
  dataService: DataService;
  chartLibrary: ChartLibrary;
  
  initialize() {
    // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ dependencies ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà inject ‡∏°‡∏≤
    const data = this.dataService.getDashboardData();
    this.chartLibrary.renderChart(data);
  }
}

// Container ‡∏à‡∏∞ inject dependencies
container.register('dashboardComponent', DashboardComponent);
container.register('dataService', DatabaseDataService);
container.register('chartLibrary', D3ChartLibrary);
```

**üéØ ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Dependency Injection:**
- **Testing:** Mock dependencies ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
- **Flexibility:** ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô implementation ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î
- **Maintainability:** Component ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö concrete classes
- **Reusability:** Component ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö dependencies ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

---

## Slide 15: üîÑ Component Communication Patterns

### ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Components

**üíª ‡πÉ‡∏ô Agent Wallboard System ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ 4 ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å:**

**1. üìû Direct Method Calls (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á)**
```javascript
// Frontend Component ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å Backend Service ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô API
class StatusManagementComponent {
  async changeStatus(newStatus) {
    // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å API endpoint ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á
    const result = await this.apiClient.post('/api/agents/status', {
      agentId: this.currentAgentId,
      status: newStatus
    });
    
    if (result.success) {
      this.updateUI(newStatus);
    }
  }
}
```
**‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠:** ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö synchronous, ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ response ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ

**2. üîî Event-Driven Communication (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Events)**
```javascript
// Publisher - Agent Status Service
class AgentStatusService {
  async updateStatus(agentId, status) {
    await this.db.updateStatus(agentId, status);
    
    // Publish event ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö
    this.eventBus.publish('agent_status_changed', {
      agentId,
      status,
      timestamp: new Date()
    });
  }
}

// Subscribers - ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ components ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ subscribe ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
class DashboardComponent {
  constructor(eventBus) {
    eventBus.subscribe('agent_status_changed', (data) => {
      this.updateDashboard(data);
    });
  }
}

class NotificationComponent {
  constructor(eventBus) {
    eventBus.subscribe('agent_status_changed', (data) => {
      this.showNotification(`Agent ${data.agentId} is now ${data.status}`);
    });
  }
}
```
**‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠:** Real-time updates, ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ components ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

**3. üì® Message Passing (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á Messages)**
```javascript
// Message Queue ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Async Processing
class MessageRoutingService {
  async sendMessage(message) {
    // ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô message queue
    await this.messageQueue.enqueue({
      type: 'SEND_MESSAGE',
      from: message.senderId,
      to: message.recipientId,
      content: message.content,
      priority: message.priority
    });
  }
}

// Background Worker
class MessageProcessor {
  async processMessages() {
    const message = await this.messageQueue.dequeue();
    
    switch (message.type) {
      case 'SEND_MESSAGE':
        await this.deliverMessage(message);
        break;
      case 'BROADCAST_MESSAGE':
        await this.broadcastToTeam(message);
        break;
    }
  }
}
```
**‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠:** Asynchronous processing, Background tasks, Load balancing

**4. üåê WebSocket Communication (Real-time Bidirectional)**
```javascript
// WebSocket Manager
class WebSocketManager {
  broadcastStatusUpdate(agentData) {
    // ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á clients ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà subscribe
    this.connectedClients.forEach(client => {
      if (client.subscriptions.includes('agent_status')) {
        client.socket.emit('agent_status_update', agentData);
      }
    });
  }
}

// Frontend WebSocket Client
class WebSocketClient {
  constructor() {
    this.socket = io.connect();
    
    this.socket.on('agent_status_update', (data) => {
      // ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ó UI ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö real-time
      this.updateAgentDisplay(data);
    });
  }
}
```
**‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠:** Real-time updates, Bidirectional communication, Live data

---

## Slide 16: üèõÔ∏è Event-Driven Architecture ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Real-time Updates

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Event-Driven

**üí° Event-Driven Architecture = ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Events ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£**

**üéØ ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å:**

**1. Event Producers (‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏ï Events)**
- Agent Status Service ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á `agent_status_changed` event
- Message Service ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á `message_sent` event  
- System Monitor ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á `system_alert` event

**2. Event Bus/Message Broker (‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡πà‡∏á)**
```javascript
class EventBus {
  constructor() {
    this.subscribers = new Map();
  }
  
  subscribe(eventType, handler) {
    if (!this.subscribers.has(eventType)) {
      this.subscribers.set(eventType, []);
    }
    this.subscribers.get(eventType).push(handler);
  }
  
  publish(eventType, eventData) {
    if (this.subscribers.has(eventType)) {
      this.subscribers.get(eventType).forEach(handler => {
        // Async execution ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà block publisher
        setImmediate(() => handler(eventData));
      });
    }
  }
  
  unsubscribe(eventType, handler) {
    if (this.subscribers.has(eventType)) {
      const handlers = this.subscribers.get(eventType);
      const index = handlers.indexOf(handler);
      if (index > -1) {
        handlers.splice(index, 1);
      }
    }
  }
}
```

**3. Event Consumers (‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Events)**
- Dashboard Components ‚Üí ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö `agent_status_changed` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ó UI
- Notification Service ‚Üí ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö events ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡πà‡∏á alerts
- Analytics Service ‚Üí ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö events ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ log ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå

**üîÑ Event Flow ‡πÉ‡∏ô Agent Wallboard System:**
```
Agent ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞
    ‚Üì
Agent Status Service receives request
    ‚Üì  
Update database
    ‚Üì
Publish 'agent_status_changed' event
    ‚Üì
Event Bus distributes to subscribers:
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Dashboard Component (‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ó UI)
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Notification Service (‡∏™‡πà‡∏á alert)
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Analytics Service (‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å log)
    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ WebSocket Manager (broadcast ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á clients)
```

**‚úÖ ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå:**
- **Decoupling:** Components ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á
- **Scalability:** ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° event consumers ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
- **Flexibility:** ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô business logic ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö producers
- **Real-time:** Events ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô

---

## Slide 17: üö™ API Gateway Pattern ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö External Communications

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏®‡∏π‡∏ô‡∏¢‡πå

**üí° API Gateway = ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö external clients ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö backend services**

**üè¢ ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö:**
- **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ Gateway:** ‡∏•‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£
- **‡∏°‡∏µ Gateway:** ‡∏•‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ

**üíª ‡πÉ‡∏ô Agent Wallboard System:**

**API Gateway Component:**
```javascript
class APIGateway {
  constructor() {
    this.authService = new AuthenticationService();
    this.agentService = new AgentStatusService();
    this.messageService = new MessageRoutingService();
    this.dashboardService = new DashboardService();
  }
  
  // Single entry point ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö external clients
  async handleRequest(request) {
    // 1. Authentication & Authorization
    const user = await this.authService.validateToken(request.token);
    if (!user) {
      return { status: 401, error: 'Unauthorized' };
    }
    
    // 2. Rate Limiting
    if (await this.isRateLimited(user.id)) {
      return { status: 429, error: 'Too many requests' };
    }
    
    // 3. Route to appropriate service
    switch (request.endpoint) {
      case '/api/agents/status':
        return await this.agentService.handleStatusRequest(request, user);
        
      case '/api/messages':
        return await this.messageService.handleMessageRequest(request, user);
        
      case '/api/dashboard':
        return await this.dashboardService.handleDashboardRequest(request, user);
        
      default:
        return { status: 404, error: 'Endpoint not found' };
    }
  }
  
  // 4. Response formatting
  formatResponse(data, format = 'json') {
    switch (format) {
      case 'json':
        return JSON.stringify(data);
      case 'xml':
        return this.convertToXML(data);
      default:
        return data;
    }
  }
}
```

**üéØ ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á API Gateway:**

**1. Authentication & Authorization**
- ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö JWT tokens
- Validate user permissions
- Session management

**2. Request Routing**
- ‡∏ô‡∏≥ request ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á backend service ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
- Load balancing ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á service instances

**3. Protocol Translation**
- ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö HTTP requests ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å clients
- ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô internal protocols (gRPC, message queues)

**4. Cross-cutting Concerns**
- Rate limiting (‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô requests)
- Logging ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ monitoring
- Error handling ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ circuit breaking

**5. Response Aggregation**
```javascript
// ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ services
async getDashboardData(userId) {
  const [agents, messages, reports] = await Promise.all([
    this.agentService.getTeamAgents(userId),
    this.messageService.getRecentMessages(userId),
    this.reportService.getKPIData(userId)
  ]);
  
  return {
    agents,
    messages,
    reports,
    lastUpdated: new Date()
  };
}
```

**‚úÖ ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå:**
- **Single Entry Point:** Clients ‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏Å endpoint ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
- **Security:** Centralized authentication/authorization
- **Monitoring:** ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° logs ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ metrics
- **Flexibility:** ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô backend services ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ clients ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ

---

## Slide 18: üìä CQRS Pattern ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Read/Write Separation

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å Command ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Query Operations

**üí° CQRS (Command Query Responsibility Segregation) = ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô (Query) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô (Command)**

**üè™ ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤:**
- **Command Side:** ‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏£‡πå (‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô, ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à) ‚Üí ‡πÄ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **Query Side:** ‡∏û‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö (‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°, ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤) ‚Üí ‡πÄ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß

**üíª ‡πÉ‡∏ô Agent Wallboard System:**

**Command Side (Write Operations):**
```javascript
class AgentStatusCommandHandler {
  constructor(database, eventBus) {
    this.db = database;  // MSSQL for ACID transactions
    this.eventBus = eventBus;
  }
  
  async handleChangeStatusCommand(command) {
    // 1. Validate command
    if (!this.isValidStatusTransition(command.oldStatus, command.newStatus)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid status transition');
    }
    
    // 2. Execute business logic
    await this.db.transaction(async (trx) => {
      await trx('agent_status_history').insert({
        agentId: command.agentId,
        oldStatus: command.oldStatus,
        newStatus: command.newStatus,
        changedBy: command.userId,
        timestamp: new Date()
      });
      
      await trx('agents').update({
        currentStatus: command.newStatus,
        lastStatusChange: new Date()
      }).where('id', command.agentId);
    });
    
    // 3. Publish event for read side
    this.eventBus.publish('agent_status_changed', {
      agentId: command.agentId,
      newStatus: command.newStatus,
      timestamp: new Date()
    });
  }
}
```

**Query Side (Read Operations):**
```javascript
class AgentStatusQueryHandler {
  constructor(readDatabase, cache) {
    this.readDb = readDatabase;  // MongoDB for fast reads
    this.cache = cache;          // Redis for ultra-fast queries
  }
  
  async getCurrentTeamStatus(teamId) {
    // 1. Try cache first
    const cached = await this.cache.get(`team_status_${teamId}`);
    if (cached) {
      return JSON.parse(cached);
    }
    
    // 2. Query read database (optimized for queries)
    const agents = await this.readDb.collection('agent_status_views')
      .find({ 
        teamId: teamId,
        active: true 
      })
      .project({
        agentId: 1,
        name: 1,
        currentStatus: 1,
        statusDuration: 1,
        lastActivity: 1
      })
      .sort({ name: 1 })
      .toArray();
    
    // 3. Cache for future requests
    await this.cache.setex(`team_status_${teamId}`, 60, JSON.stringify(agents));
    
    return agents;
  }
  
  async getStatusHistory(agentId, dateRange) {
    // Complex analytical query - optimized read model
    return await this.readDb.collection('agent_status_analytics')
      .aggregate([
        { $match: { agentId, date: { $gte: dateRange.start, $lte: dateRange.end } } },
        { $group: {
            _id: '$status',
            totalDuration: { $sum: '$durationMinutes' },
            count: { $sum: 1 }
          }
        }
      ]).toArray();
  }
}
```

**üîÑ CQRS Flow ‡πÉ‡∏ô Agent Wallboard System:**
```
Agent ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞ (Command)
    ‚Üì
Command Handler:
  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Validate business rules
  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Update MSSQL (ACID transaction)
  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Publish event
    ‚Üì
Event Handler ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ó Read Models:
  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ MongoDB views ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö queries
  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Redis cache ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö real-time data
  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Analytics database ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
    ‚Üì
Dashboard queries (Query Side):
  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Read from optimized MongoDB collections
  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Use Redis cache ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢
```

**‚úÖ ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á CQRS:**
- **Performance:** ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å optimize read/write operations
- **Scalability:** Scale read ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ write ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô
- **Flexibility:** Read models ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° UI requirements
- **Consistency:** Write side ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô business rules

**‚ö†Ô∏è ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏≤:**
- **Complexity:** ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô
- **Eventual Consistency:** Read side ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢
- **Data Synchronization:** ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á sync ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á write/read sides

---

## Slide 19: üîß Component Interface Design

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Interface ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û

**üí° Component Interface = ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Components**

**üéØ ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Interface:**

**1. Clear and Descriptive Naming**
```javascript
// ‚úÖ Good naming
interface AgentStatusService {
  getCurrentStatus(agentId: string): Promise<AgentStatus>;
  updateStatus(agentId: string, newStatus: StatusType): Promise<void>;
  getStatusHistory(agentId: string, dateRange: DateRange): Promise<StatusHistory[]>;
}

// ‚ùå Poor naming  
interface AgentService {
  get(id: string): Promise<any>;
  set(id: string, data: any): Promise<void>;
  list(params: any): Promise<any[]>;
}
```

**2. Single Responsibility per Interface**
```javascript
// ‚úÖ Focused interfaces
interface MessageSender {
  sendMessage(message: Message): Promise<MessageResult>;
  sendBroadcast(message: Message, recipients: string[]): Promise<BroadcastResult>;
}

interface MessageRetriever {
  getMessage(messageId: string): Promise<Message>;
  getMessageHistory(userId: string, limit: number): Promise<Message[]>;
}

interface MessageValidator {
  validateMessage(message: Message): ValidationResult;
  sanitizeContent(content: string): string;
}

// ‚ùå Mixed responsibilities
interface MessageManager {
  sendMessage(message: Message): Promise<MessageResult>;
  getMessage(messageId: string): Promise<Message>;
  validateMessage(message: Message): ValidationResult;
  generateReport(): Promise<Report>;
  backupMessages(): Promise<void>;
}
```

**3. Consistent Error Handling**
```javascript
// Standardized error response
interface APIResponse<T> {
  success: boolean;
  data?: T;
  error?: {
    code: string;
    message: string;
    details?: any;
  };
  metadata?: {
    timestamp: Date;
    requestId: string;
  };
}

// Usage in interface
interface AgentStatusService {
  updateStatus(agentId: string, status: StatusType): Promise<APIResponse<void>>;
  getCurrentStatus(agentId: string): Promise<APIResponse<AgentStatus>>;
}
```

**4. Versioning Strategy**
```javascript
// Interface versioning
interface AgentStatusServiceV1 {
  updateStatus(agentId: string, status: string): Promise<void>;
}

interface AgentStatusServiceV2 {
  updateStatus(agentId: string, status: StatusType, reason?: string): Promise<void>;
  updateStatusWithValidation(request: StatusUpdateRequest): Promise<StatusUpdateResult>;
}

// Backward compatibility
class AgentStatusServiceAdapter implements AgentStatusServiceV1, AgentStatusServiceV2 {
  // Implement both versions
}
```

**üîÑ Interface Examples for Agent Wallboard System:**

**Authentication Interface:**
```javascript
interface AuthenticationService {
  // Core authentication
  authenticate(credentials: LoginCredentials): Promise<AuthenticationResult>;
  validateToken(token: string): Promise<TokenValidationResult>;
  refreshToken(refreshToken: string): Promise<TokenRefreshResult>;
  
  // Session management
  createSession(userId: string): Promise<Session>;
  getSession(sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null>;
  destroySession(sessionId: string): Promise<void>;
}

interface LoginCredentials {
  username: string;
  password: string;
  authMethod: 'local' | 'sso' | 'ldap';
}

interface AuthenticationResult {
  success: boolean;
  user?: User;
  accessToken?: string;
  refreshToken?: string;
  expiresIn?: number;
  error?: string;
}
```

**Dashboard Interface:**
```javascript
interface DashboardService {
  // Data retrieval
  getDashboardData(userId: string, filters?: DashboardFilters): Promise<DashboardData>;
  getAgentSummary(teamId: string): Promise<AgentSummary>;
  getPerformanceMetrics(teamId: string, period: TimePeriod): Promise<PerformanceMetrics>;
  
  // Real-time subscriptions
  subscribeToDashboardUpdates(userId: string, callback: (update: DashboardUpdate) => void): void;
  unsubscribeFromDashboardUpdates(userId: string): void;
}

interface DashboardData {
  agents: AgentStatus[];
  teamMetrics: TeamMetrics;
  alerts: SystemAlert[];
  lastUpdated: Date;
}
```

## Slide 20: ‚úÖ Interface Design Best Practices

### ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Interface

**üéØ Best Practices ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Agent Wallboard System:**

**1. Use TypeScript/Strong Typing**
```typescript
// Define precise types
type AgentStatusType = 'Available' | 'Busy' | 'Away' | 'Break' | 'Offline';
type MessagePriority = 'Low' | 'Normal' | 'High' | 'Critical';

interface StatusUpdateRequest {
  agentId: string;
  newStatus: AgentStatusType;
  reason?: string;
  scheduledTime?: Date;  // For scheduled status changes
}

interface MessageRequest {
  senderId: string;
  recipientIds: string[];
  content: string;
  priority: MessagePriority;
  attachments?: FileAttachment[];
}
```

**2. Provide Default Values and Optional Parameters**
```typescript
interface DashboardQueryOptions {
  teamId?: string;           // Optional - default to user's team
  statusFilter?: AgentStatusType[];  // Optional - default to all statuses
  limit?: number;            // Optional - default to 50
  sortBy?: 'name' | 'status' | 'lastActivity';  // Optional - default to 'name'
  includeInactive?: boolean;  // Optional - default to false
}

// Implementation with defaults
async getDashboardData(userId: string, options: DashboardQueryOptions = {}): Promise<DashboardData> {
  const {
    teamId = await this.getUserTeam(userId),
    statusFilter = ['Available', 'Busy', 'Away', 'Break'],
    limit = 50,
    sortBy = 'name',
    includeInactive = false
  } = options;
  
  // Implementation...
}
```

**3. Design for Extensibility**
```typescript
// Base interface
interface BaseMessage {
  id: string;
  senderId: string;
  recipientId: string;
  content: string;
  timestamp: Date;
  type: string;
}

// Extended interfaces
interface ChatMessage extends BaseMessage {
  type: 'chat';
  attachments?: FileAttachment[];
}

interface SystemAlert extends BaseMessage {
  type: 'alert';
  severity: 'info' | 'warning' | 'error';
  actionRequired: boolean;
}

interface StatusNotification extends BaseMessage {
  type: 'status';
  agentId: string;
  oldStatus: AgentStatusType;
  newStatus: AgentStatusType;
}

// Union type for all message types
type Message = ChatMessage | SystemAlert | StatusNotification;

// Service interface that can handle all types
interface MessageService {
  sendMessage<T extends Message>(message: T): Promise<void>;
  getMessages(userId: string): Promise<Message[]>;
}
```

**4. Include Metadata and Context**
```typescript
interface ServiceResponse<T> {
  data: T;
  metadata: {
    requestId: string;
    timestamp: Date;
    processingTime: number;
    version: string;
  };
  pagination?: {
    total: number;
    page: number;
    pageSize: number;
    hasNext: boolean;
  };
}

interface AgentStatusHistory {
  agentId: string;
  statusChanges: StatusChange[];
  summary: {
    totalDuration: number;
    mostCommonStatus: AgentStatusType;
    statusDistribution: Record<AgentStatusType, number>;
  };
  queryInfo: {
    dateRange: DateRange;
    generatedAt: Date;
    dataSource: 'live' | 'cached' | 'historical';
  };
}
```

**5. Error Handling Patterns**
```typescript
// Custom error types
class ValidationError extends Error {
  constructor(field: string, message: string) {
    super(`Validation error in ${field}: ${message}`);
    this.name = 'ValidationError';
  }
}

class BusinessRuleError extends Error {
  constructor(rule: string, context: any) {
    super(`Business rule violated: ${rule}`);
    this.name = 'BusinessRuleError';
    this.context = context;
  }
}

// Interface with proper error handling
interface AgentStatusService {
  updateStatus(request: StatusUpdateRequest): Promise<Result<void, ValidationError | BusinessRuleError>>;
}

// Result type for better error handling
type Result<T, E> = {
  success: true;
  data: T;
} | {
  success: false;
  error: E;
};

// Usage
const result = await agentStatusService.updateStatus(request);
if (result.success) {
  console.log('Status updated successfully');
} else {
  if (result.error instanceof ValidationError) {
    // Handle validation error
  } else if (result.error instanceof BusinessRuleError) {
    // Handle business rule error
  }
}
```

**üí° Key Takeaways:**
- **Interfaces ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ç‡∏≤** ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Components
- **Type safety** ‡∏•‡∏î bugs ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ô‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠
- **Consistency** ‡πÉ‡∏ô naming ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ patterns
- **Extensibility** ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ï
- **Error handling** ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

# ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 7: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ã‡∏≠‡∏ü‡∏ï‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πå - ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô (Part 3/4)
## Component Communication ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Architecture Patterns

---

## Slide 21: üé® ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á C3 Component Diagram - ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö

### ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û Components ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Agent Wallboard System

**üéØ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á C3 Diagram:**

**Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ Components ‡πÉ‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Container**
```
Desktop App Container:
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Authentication Component
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Status Management Component  
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Notification Component
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Profile Component
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ WebSocket Client Component

API Server Container:
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Authentication Service
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Agent Status Service
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Message Routing Service
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ WebSocket Manager
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Database Access Layer
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Event Bus Component

Database Container:
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ MSSQL Component
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ MongoDB Component
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Connection Pool Manager
```

**Step 2: ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Interface ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Components**
```
Authentication Component ‚Üí Authentication Service
  Interface: POST /api/auth/login, GET /api/auth/validate

Status Management ‚Üí Agent Status Service  
  Interface: PUT /api/agents/{id}/status, GET /api/agents/{id}/status

WebSocket Client ‚Üî WebSocket Manager
  Interface: agent_status_update, message_received, system_alert

Database Access Layer ‚Üí MSSQL/MongoDB
  Interface: SQL queries, MongoDB operations
```

**Step 3: ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á Dependencies ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Data Flow**
```
User Input (Status Change)
    ‚Üì
Status Management Component
    ‚Üì HTTP Request
Agent Status Service  
    ‚Üì Database Query
Database Access Layer
    ‚Üì SQL/NoSQL
MSSQL/MongoDB
    ‚Üë Response
Database Access Layer
    ‚Üë Service Response  
Agent Status Service
    ‚Üì WebSocket Event
WebSocket Manager
    ‚Üì Real-time Update
All Connected Clients
```

**Step 4: ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà Technology Details**
- **Communication Protocols:** HTTP/HTTPS, WebSocket, TCP/IP
- **Data Formats:** JSON, SQL Results, MongoDB Documents
- **Authentication:** JWT Tokens, Session Management
- **Error Handling:** Circuit Breaker, Retry Logic

## Slide 22: üìä C3 Diagram - Desktop App Components

### ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î Components ‡πÉ‡∏ô Desktop Application

**üñ•Ô∏è Agent Desktop App (Electron.js Container):**

```
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ               Desktop Application               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                 (Electron.js)                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê    ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ  Authentication ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ   Status Management   ‚îÇ‚îÇ

**üîó Component Interactions:**

**Authentication Component:**
- **Interface:** IAuthentication
- **Dependencies:** API Client, Session Storage
- **Responsibilities:** User login/logout, token management

**Status Management Component:**
- **Interface:** IStatusManager  
- **Dependencies:** Authentication, API Client, WebSocket Client
- **Responsibilities:** Agent status changes, status history

**WebSocket Client Component:**
- **Interface:** IWebSocketClient
- **Dependencies:** Authentication (for connection auth)
- **Responsibilities:** Real-time communication, event handling

**Notification Component:**
- **Interface:** INotificationDisplay
- **Dependencies:** WebSocket Client
- **Responsibilities:** Show alerts, messages, status updates

**Profile Component:**
- **Interface:** IProfile
- **Dependencies:** Authentication, API Client
- **Responsibilities:** User preferences, settings management

---

**üîó Supervisor Dashboard Component Details:**

**Dashboard Visualization Component:**
- **Renders:** Real-time charts, KPI metrics, team overview
- **Updates:** Every 5 seconds via WebSocket
- **Libraries:** Chart.js, D3.js ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö data visualization

**Agent Monitor Component:**  
- **Displays:** Individual agent status, performance metrics
- **Features:** Filter, search, drill-down capabilities
- **Real-time:** Live status updates, activity tracking

**Message Management Component:**
- **Functions:** Send messages to agents, broadcast announcements
- **Message Types:** Individual chat, team broadcast, urgent alerts
- **History:** Message tracking, delivery confirmation

**Reports Component:**
- **Generates:** Daily/weekly/monthly reports
- **Formats:** PDF, Excel, CSV export
- **Scheduling:** Automated report generation

**Control Panel Component:**
- **Administration:** Team settings, user management
- **Configuration:** System settings, alert thresholds
- **Audit:** Activity logs, security monitoring

‚îÇ           ‚îÇ                   ‚îÇ                 ‚îÇ

‚îÇ ‚îÇ   WebSocket     ‚îÇ‚óÑ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îº‚îÄ‚ñ∫‚îÇ   Message    ‚îÇ‚îÇ

‚îÇ ‚îÇ                 ‚îÇ          ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ   Service    ‚îÇ‚îÇ

‚îÇ ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò          ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ‚Ä¢ persist()   ‚îÇ‚îÇ

‚îÇ           ‚îÇ                  ‚îÇ                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ        Database Access Layer                ‚îÇ ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ                                             ‚îÇ ‚îÇ

‚îÇ ‚îÇ‚Ä¢ insertDocument(collection, doc)            ‚îÇ ‚îÇ

‚îÇ ‚îÇ‚Ä¢ getConnection(type)                        ‚îÇ ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò ‚îÇ

                           ‚îÇ
                           ‚ñº SQL/NoSQL
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ              Database Layer                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ        (MSSQL + MongoDB)                        ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
```

**‚öôÔ∏è API Server Component Details:**

**Authentication Service:**
- **Strategies:** Local, SSO, LDAP (Strategy Pattern)
- **Token Management:** JWT creation, validation, refresh
- **Session Handling:** Create, validate, destroy sessions

**Agent Status Service:**
- **Business Logic:** Status transition validation
- **Data Operations:** CRUD operations for agent status
- **Event Publishing:** Broadcast status changes via Event Bus

**Message Routing Service:**
- **Routing Logic:** Individual messages, team broadcasts
- **Message Types:** Chat, alerts, announcements (Factory Pattern)
- **Persistence:** Store message history, delivery tracking

**WebSocket Manager:**
- **Connection Management:** Handle connections, disconnections
- **Room Management:** Group users by teams, roles
- **Broadcasting:** Send real-time updates to relevant clients

**Event Bus Component:**
- **Pub-Sub Pattern:** Decouple components via events
- **Event Types:** status_changed, message_sent, user_login
- **Reliability:** Ensure event delivery, handle failures

**Database Access Layer:**
- **Abstraction:** Hide database specifics from services
- **Connection Pooling:** Efficient database connection management
- **Transaction Management:** ACID transactions for critical operations

‚îÇ           ‚îÇ            ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê‚îÇ
‚îÇ           ‚îÇ            ‚îÇ     MongoDB           ‚îÇ‚îÇ
‚îÇ           ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚ñ∫‚îÇ    Component          ‚îÇ‚îÇ

```

**üîê Database Component Responsibilities:**

**MSSQL Component:**
- **Master Data:** Agent profiles, team structures, user accounts
- **Configuration:** System settings, business rules
- **Referential Integrity:** Foreign key constraints, data consistency
- **ACID Transactions:** Critical business operations

**MongoDB Component:**  
- **Real-time Data:** Agent status logs, live activity tracking
- **Message Storage:** Chat history, broadcast messages
- **Analytics Data:** Performance metrics, usage statistics
- **Flexible Schema:** Adaptable document structure

**Data Synchronization Component:**
- **Two-way Sync:** Keep MSSQL and MongoDB consistent  
- **Conflict Resolution:** Handle simultaneous updates
- **Change Detection:** Track data modifications
- **Audit Trail:** Log all synchronization activities

**Connection Pool Manager:**
- **Resource Management:** Optimize database connections
- **Load Balancing:** Distribute queries across instances
- **Health Monitoring:** Track connection status
- **Failover:** Handle database unavailability

**Data Security Component:**
- **Encryption:** Protect sensitive data at rest
- **Access Control:** Role-based database permissions  
- **Audit Logging:** Track all data access
- **Compliance:** Meet security standards

## Slide 26: üîÑ Component Interaction Flow

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Components

**üìä Complete Interaction Flow - Agent Status Change:**

```
1. User Input (Agent Desktop)
   ‚îÇ
   ‚ñº
2. Status Management Component
   ‚îÇ validateInput()
   ‚îÇ showLoading()
   ‚ñº
3. HTTP API Call to Backend
   ‚îÇ PUT /api/agents/{id}/status
   ‚îÇ Authorization: Bearer <token>
   ‚ñº
4. Authentication Service
   ‚îÇ validateToken()
   ‚îÇ checkPermissions()
   ‚ñº
5. Agent Status Service  
   ‚îÇ validateStatusTransition()
   ‚îÇ checkBusinessRules()
   ‚ñº
6. Database Access Layer
   ‚îÇ beginTransaction()
   ‚îÇ updateAgentStatus()
   ‚îÇ logStatusHistory()
   ‚îÇ commitTransaction()
   ‚ñº
7. Event Bus Publishing
   ‚îÇ publish('agent_status_changed', data)
   ‚ñº
8. Multiple Subscribers:
   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ WebSocket Manager
   ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ broadcastToSupervisors()
   ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ broadcastToTeam()
   ‚îÇ   ‚ñº
   ‚îÇ   Supervisor Dashboard
   ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ updateUI()
   ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ playNotificationSound()
   ‚îÇ
   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Analytics Service
   ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ recordMetric()
   ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ updatePerformanceData()
   ‚îÇ
   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Notification Service
       ‚îÇ sendEmailAlert() (if configured)
       ‚îÇ sendSMSAlert() (if critical)
```

**‚è±Ô∏è Timing and Performance:**

**Synchronous Operations (< 200ms):**
- Input validation
- Token authentication
- Business rule checking
- Database updates

**Asynchronous Operations (background):**
- Event broadcasting
- Analytics recording  
- Email/SMS notifications
- Report generation

**Real-time Updates (< 1 second):**
- WebSocket broadcasts
- UI updates
- Dashboard refreshes

## Slide 27: üìã Component Dependencies Matrix

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå Dependencies ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Components

**üìä Dependency Matrix for Agent Wallboard System:**

| Component | Auth Service | Agent Status Service | Message Service | WebSocket Manager | Database Layer | Event Bus |
|-----------|:------------:|:-------------------:|:--------------:|:----------------:|:-------------:|:---------:|
| **Authentication Component** | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚ùå |
| **Status Management Component** | ‚úÖ Indirect | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚ùå | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚ùå | ‚ùå |
| **Notification Component** | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚ùå | ‚ùå |
| **Dashboard Component** | ‚úÖ Indirect | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚ùå | ‚ùå |
| **Auth Service** | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚úÖ Direct |
| **Agent Status Service** | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚úÖ Direct |
| **Message Service** | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚úÖ Direct |
| **WebSocket Manager** | ‚úÖ Direct | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚ùå | ‚úÖ Direct |

**üîç Dependency Analysis:**

**‚úÖ Good Dependencies (Following Architecture Rules):**
- Frontend components depend on Backend services ‚úì
- Services depend on Database layer ‚úì  
- All services use Event Bus for decoupling ‚úì
- Authentication is used by components that need it ‚úì

**‚ö†Ô∏è Potential Issues:**
- **WebSocket Manager** has many incoming dependencies
- **Event Bus** is a central point of failure
- **Database Layer** is heavily used (potential bottleneck)

**üõ†Ô∏è Mitigation Strategies:**

**For WebSocket Manager:**
```javascript
// Use connection pooling and load balancing
class WebSocketManager {
  constructor() {
    this.connectionPools = new Map();
    this.loadBalancer = new RoundRobinLoadBalancer();
  }
  
  broadcast(event, data) {
    const pool = this.loadBalancer.getNextPool();
    return pool.broadcast(event, data);
  }
}
```

**For Event Bus Reliability:**
```javascript
// Implement circuit breaker and fallback
class ResilientEventBus {
  constructor() {
    this.circuitBreaker = new CircuitBreaker();
    this.fallbackQueue = new InMemoryQueue();
  }
  
  async publish(event, data) {
    try {
      await this.circuitBreaker.execute(() => 
        this.eventBus.publish(event, data)
      );
    } catch (error) {
      // Fallback to in-memory queue
      this.fallbackQueue.enqueue({event, data});
    }
  }
}
```

**For Database Layer:**
```javascript  
// Implement connection pooling and caching
class DatabaseAccessLayer {
  constructor() {
    this.connectionPool = new ConnectionPool();
    this.cache = new RedisCache();
  }
  
  async query(sql, params) {
    // Check cache first
    const cacheKey = this.generateCacheKey(sql, params);
    let result = await this.cache.get(cacheKey);
    
    if (!result) {
      const connection = await this.connectionPool.getConnection();
      result = await connection.query(sql, params);
      await this.cache.set(cacheKey, result, 300); // 5 min TTL
    }
    
    return result;
  }
}
```

---

## Slide 28: üö® Common Anti-Patterns ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Solutions

### ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Components

**‚ùå Common Anti-Patterns:**

**1. God Component (Component ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ)**
```javascript
// ‚ùå Anti-pattern: ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á
class SuperManagerComponent {
  // Authentication
  login() { }
  logout() { }
  
  // Agent Management  
  updateAgentStatus() { }
  getAgentList() { }
  
  // Messaging
  sendMessage() { }
  broadcastAnnouncement() { }
  
  // Reporting
  generateReport() { }
  exportToPDF() { }
  
  // Database
  connectToDatabase() { }
  executeQuery() { }
  
  // UI Management
  renderDashboard() { }
  updateCharts() { }
}
```

**‚úÖ Solution: ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å Components ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Single Responsibility**
```javascript
// ‚úÖ Separate responsibilities
class AuthenticationComponent {
  login() { }
  logout() { }
  validateSession() { }
}

class AgentManagementComponent {
  updateAgentStatus() { }
  getAgentList() { }
  monitorAgents() { }
}

class MessagingComponent {
  sendMessage() { }
  broadcastAnnouncement() { }
  getMessageHistory() { }
}
```

**2. Circular Dependencies (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ß‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏°)**
```javascript
// ‚ùå Anti-pattern: A depends on B, B depends on A
class ComponentA {
  constructor(componentB) {
    this.b = componentB;
  }
  
  doSomething() {
    this.b.helpMe(); // A uses B
  }
}

class ComponentB {
  constructor(componentA) {
    this.a = componentA;
  }
  
  helpMe() {
    this.a.doSomethingElse(); // B uses A - CIRCULAR!
  }
}
```

**‚úÖ Solution: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Event Bus ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Mediator Pattern**
```javascript
// ‚úÖ Break circular dependency with Event Bus
class ComponentA {
  constructor(eventBus) {
    this.eventBus = eventBus;
  }
  
  doSomething() {
    this.eventBus.publish('need_help', { from: 'A', data: '...' });
  }
}

class ComponentB {
  constructor(eventBus) {
    this.eventBus = eventBus;
    this.eventBus.subscribe('need_help', (event) => {
      if (event.from === 'A') {
        this.provideHelp(event.data);
      }
    });
  }
  
  provideHelp(data) {
    // Help without direct dependency on A
    this.eventBus.publish('help_provided', { to: 'A', result: '...' });
  }
}
```

**3. Hidden Dependencies (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà)**
```javascript
// ‚ùå Anti-pattern: Hidden global dependencies
class UserService {
  getUser(id) {
    // Hidden dependency on global database connection
    return window.database.query(`SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = ${id}`);
  }
  
  sendEmail(user, message) {
    // Hidden dependency on global email service
    return window.emailService.send(user.email, message);
  }
}
```

**‚úÖ Solution: Explicit Dependency Injection**
```javascript
// ‚úÖ Make dependencies explicit
class UserService {
  constructor(database, emailService) {
    this.database = database;
    this.emailService = emailService;
  }
  
  async getUser(id) {
    return await this.database.query('users').find({ id });
  }
  
  async sendEmail(user, message) {
    return await this.emailService.send({
      to: user.email,
      subject: message.subject,
      body: message.body
    });
  }
}

// Clear instantiation with dependencies
const userService = new UserService(
  new DatabaseConnection(),
  new EmailService()
);
```

**4. Tight Coupling Through Concrete Classes**
```javascript
// ‚ùå Anti-pattern: Depend on concrete implementations
class OrderProcessor {
  constructor() {
    this.emailSender = new SMTPEmailSender(); // Hardcoded concrete class
    this.paymentGateway = new PayPalGateway(); // Hardcoded concrete class
  }
  
  processOrder(order) {
    const payment = this.paymentGateway.charge(order.total);
    this.emailSender.send(order.customerEmail, 'Order confirmed');
  }
}
```

**‚úÖ Solution: Depend on Interfaces/Abstractions**
```javascript
// ‚úÖ Depend on interfaces
class OrderProcessor {
  constructor(emailSender, paymentGateway) {
    this.emailSender = emailSender; // Interface: IEmailSender
    this.paymentGateway = paymentGateway; // Interface: IPaymentGateway
  }
  
  async processOrder(order) {
    const payment = await this.paymentGateway.charge(order.total);
    await this.emailSender.send(order.customerEmail, 'Order confirmed');
  }
}

// Different implementations can be injected
const orderProcessor = new OrderProcessor(
  new SMTPEmailSender(),    // or SendGridEmailSender, AWSEmailSender
  new PayPalGateway()       // or StripeGateway, SquareGateway
);
```

**üéØ Key Takeaways:**
- **Single Responsibility:** ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á component ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà
- **Explicit Dependencies:** ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô dependencies
- **Interface-based Design:** ‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤ abstractions ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà concrete classes
- **Event-driven Communication:** ‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á

---

## Slide 29: ‚úÖ Component Design Checklist

### ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Components

**üìã Component Design Quality Checklist:**

**üéØ Single Responsibility Principle:**
- [ ] Component ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô
- [ ] ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å method ‡πÉ‡∏ô component ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô
- [ ] ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ component ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ "‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞" ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ "‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠"
- [ ] ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ôÊ•≠Âãô requirement ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö component ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß

**üîó Dependency Management:**
- [ ] Dependencies ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å inject ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà new ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô)
- [ ] ‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤ interfaces/abstractions ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà concrete classes
- [ ] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ circular dependencies
- [ ] ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô dependencies ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 5 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ component

**üé≠ Interface Design:**
- [ ] Interface ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
- [ ] Method names ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô verb ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥
- [ ] Parameters ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ return types ‡∏°‡∏µ strong typing
- [ ] Error handling ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

**üì¶ Encapsulation:**
- [ ] ‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î implementation ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ
- [ ] Public interface ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô
- [ ] Internal state ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á
- [ ] Immutable objects ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

**üß™ Testability:**
- [ ] Component ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ unit test ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô
- [ ] Dependencies ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ mock ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
- [ ] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤ external resources ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ test
- [ ] Test coverage ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢ 80%

**üìä Performance Considerations:**
- [ ] Component ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô
- [ ] ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ cache ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°
- [ ] Lazy loading ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö expensive operations
- [ ] Memory leaks ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (cleanup resources)

**Agent Wallboard System Specific Checklist:**

**Real-time Components:**
- [ ] WebSocket connections ‡∏°‡∏µ reconnection logic
- [ ] Event handlers ‡∏°‡∏µ error boundaries
- [ ] Real-time updates ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà block UI thread
- [ ] ‡∏°‡∏µ fallback mechanism ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ connection ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏î

**Authentication Components:**
- [ ] Tokens ‡∏°‡∏µ expiration handling
- [ ] Session timeout ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô
- [ ] Sensitive data ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ô localStorage
- [ ] Multi-factor authentication support

**Status Management:**
- [ ] Status transitions ‡∏°‡∏µ validation
- [ ] Status history ‡∏°‡∏µ audit trail
- [ ] Concurrent status changes ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
- [ ] Status conflicts ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ resolve

**Message Components:**
- [ ] Message delivery ‡∏°‡∏µ confirmation
- [ ] Message priority ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
- [ ] Message history ‡∏°‡∏µ pagination
- [ ] Offline messages ‡∏°‡∏µ queue mechanism

## Slide 30: üéØ Component Architecture Summary

### ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Component Architecture

**üèÜ Key Principles ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ:**

**1. üß© Component-Based Thinking**
- **‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:** ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ component ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ä‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
- **Interface-driven:** ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö interface ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô implementation
- **Reusable:** Component ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ

**2. üîó Dependency Management**
- **Loose Coupling:** Components ‡∏û‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
- **Dependency Injection:** ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á dependencies ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å
- **Interface Segregation:** ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å interface ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏á

**3. üì° Communication Patterns**
- **Event-Driven:** ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ events ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö real-time communication
- **API Gateway:** ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö external clients
- **CQRS:** ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å read ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ write operations ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ performance

**4. üèóÔ∏è Architecture Patterns**
- **Layered Architecture:** ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ä‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° responsibilities
- **Component Composition:** ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° components ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà
- **Pattern Integration:** ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ design patterns ‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö components

**üìä Agent Wallboard System Architecture Overview:**

```
Frontend Tier (Components):
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Authentication Component
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Status Management Component  
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Dashboard Visualization Component
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Message Management Component
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Real-time Notification Component
                    ‚Üì HTTP/WebSocket
Backend Tier (Services):
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Authentication Service
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Agent Status Service
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Message Routing Service
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ WebSocket Connection Manager
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Event Bus Component
                    ‚Üì Database Queries
Data Tier (Components):
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ MSSQL Component (Master Data)
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ MongoDB Component (Real-time Data)
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Connection Pool Manager
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Data Synchronization Component
```

**üéØ Benefits ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö:**
- **Maintainability:** ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç component ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô
- **Scalability:** Scale components ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° load
- **Testability:** Test ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ component ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
- **Team Productivity:** ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å components ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
- **Technology Flexibility:** ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏Ñ‡πÇ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á component ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

**üöÄ Next Steps ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤:**
- **C4 Level 4 (Code):** Class diagrams, sequence diagrams
- **API Design:** REST endpoints, WebSocket events
- **Database Design:** Schema design, relationships
- **Implementation Planning:** Sprint planning, task breakdown

**üîß Tools ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤:**
- **Diagram Tools:** Draw.io, Lucidchart, PlantUML
- **Code Structure:** TypeScript interfaces, JSDoc
- **Testing:** Jest, Mocha, Postman
- **Documentation:** Swagger/OpenAPI, README files

   - ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ functional requirements

   Responsibility: ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ login/logout ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ session management

   - ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ components ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ
   - ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á dependency (composition, aggregation)
   - ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á circular dependencies

   - Protocol ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ (HTTP, WebSocket, Function calls)
   - Data format (JSON, Objects, Events)
   - Error handling mechanism

- **Draw.io** (diagrams.net) - ‡∏ü‡∏£‡∏µ, ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢

- **PlantUML** - ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡∏≠‡∏ö text-based

3. **Dependency Analysis** (Table/List)

## Slide 32: üìù Workshop Guidelines ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Templates

### ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥ Workshop

**üìã Component Interface Template:**

```typescript
// Component Interface Template
interface ComponentName {
  // Primary Functions
  primaryFunction(param1: Type1, param2: Type2): Promise<ReturnType>;
  
  // Secondary Functions  
  secondaryFunction(param: Type): ReturnType;
  
  // Event Handlers (if applicable)
  onEventName(callback: (data: EventData) => void): void;
  
  // Lifecycle Methods (if applicable)
  initialize(): Promise<void>;
  cleanup(): Promise<void>;
}

// Data Types
interface InputType {
  property1: string;
  property2: number;
  optionalProperty?: boolean;
}

interface ReturnType {
  success: boolean;
  data?: any;
  error?: string;
}
```

**üé® Component Diagram Elements:**

**Component Representation:**
```
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ   Component Name    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ‚Ä¢ publicMethod1()    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ‚Ä¢ publicMethod2()    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ‚Ä¢ publicMethod3()    ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
```

**Relationship Types:**
- **‚Üí** Uses/Calls (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô services)
- **‚Üê‚Üí** Bidirectional (‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á)
- **‚áí** Events (‡∏™‡πà‡∏á events)
- **‚ü¶‚üß** Contains (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ sub-components)

**üìã Component Specification Markdown format Example:**

```markdown
## Authentication Component

### Purpose
‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ authentication ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ session management ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö desktop application

### Interface
```typescript
interface IAuthentication {
  login(credentials: LoginCredentials): Promise<AuthResult>;
  logout(): Promise<void>;
  validateSession(): Promise<boolean>;
  getCurrentUser(): User | null;
  refreshToken(): Promise<string>;
}
```

### Dependencies
- API Client (HTTP requests)
- Session Storage (token persistence)
- Event Bus (authentication events)

### Events Published
- `user_login`: ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ user login ‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à
- `user_logout`: ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ user logout
- `session_expired`: ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ session ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏

### Error Handling
- `AuthenticationError`: ‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î
- `NetworkError`: ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠
- `SessionExpiredError`: Session ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏
```

## Slide 34: üìä Workshop Assessment Criteria

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ standard notation ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ best practices

- Relationships ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

**Satisfactory (24-29 ‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô):**

**Needs Improvement (0-23 ‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô):**

## Slide 37: üöÄ Next Week Preparation

### ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 8

**üìÖ ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 8: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ã‡∏≠‡∏ü‡∏ï‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πå - ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á**

**üîó ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:**

**‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß (Week 7):**
- ‚úÖ C3 Component Diagram ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Component breakdown
- ‚úÖ Component Design Principles (High Cohesion, Loose Coupling)
- ‚úÖ Interface Segregation ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Dependency Injection
- ‚úÖ Communication Patterns (Event-driven, API Gateway, CQRS)

**‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ (Week 8):**
- üöÄ **C4 Level 4 (Code):** Class Diagrams, Method Details
- üöÄ **UML Diagrams:** Sequence, Activity, State Diagrams
- üöÄ **API Specifications:** REST endpoints, WebSocket protocols
- üöÄ **Database Design:** Schema, relationships, optimization

**üìö ‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏•‡∏á‡∏•‡∏∂‡∏Å:**

**1. C4 Model Level 4 - Code Level Design**
```javascript
// From high-level components to actual classes
class AgentStatusManager {
  private database: IDatabase;
  private eventBus: IEventBus;
  
  constructor(database: IDatabase, eventBus: IEventBus) {
    this.database = database;
    this.eventBus = eventBus;
  }
  
  async updateStatus(agentId: string, status: StatusType): Promise<void> {
    await this.database.updateAgentStatus(agentId, status);
    this.eventBus.publish('agent_status_changed', { agentId, status });
  }
}
```

**2. UML Sequence Diagrams**
```
Agent -> StatusComponent: changeStatus("Busy")
StatusComponent -> AuthService: validatePermission()
AuthService --> StatusComponent: authorized
StatusComponent -> AgentService: updateStatus(agentId, "Busy")
AgentService -> Database: UPDATE agents SET status = "Busy"
Database --> AgentService: success
AgentService -> EventBus: publish("status_changed")
EventBus -> Dashboard: notify(statusUpdate)
Dashboard --> Agent: statusUpdated()
```

**3. API Design Specifications**
```yaml
# OpenAPI/Swagger specification
paths:
  /api/agents/{agentId}/status:
    put:
      summary: Update agent status
      parameters:
        - name: agentId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              properties:
                status:
                  type: string
                  enum: [Available, Busy, Away, Break, Offline]
                reason:
                  type: string
      responses:
        200:
          description: Status updated successfully
        400:
          description: Invalid status transition
        401:
          description: Unauthorized
```

**üîß ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤:**

**Tools ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á:**
- **PlantUML** ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö UML diagrams
- **Swagger Editor** ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö API design
- **DB Designer** (draw.io database plugin)
- **Postman** ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö API testing

**Knowledge ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ß‡∏ô:**

- **JSON Schema:** ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö API documentation
